  488. # [05:58] <@roc> right
  489. # [05:59] <@khuey|tw> it depends on the reactor design
  490. # [05:59] <@khuey|tw> in typical light water reactors the moderator slows down the neutrons enough to let them actually react with the fissile material
  491. # [05:59] <@khuey|tw> if you drain the water from a typical LWR the fission will stop
  492. # [05:59] <@khuey|tw> the neutrons are too energetic to actually cause fission, they just bounce right off
  493. # [06:00] <@khuey|tw> the melting a hole in the ground is because of the radioactive decay of the fission products, not an actual continuing fission reaction
